[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo understand the full scope of this vulnerability, the following components should[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe thoroughly examined:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Investigation Area - `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m`:**[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m in the `json_parse_ex` function where the out-of-bounds read occurs[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m958[0m[39m in the `json_parse` function that calls `json_parse_ex`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Buffer management logic in JSON parsing routines[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - String/buffer length validation mechanisms[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Boundary checking before memory access operations[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Harness - `[0m[35m/src/[0m[95mjson_fuzz.c[0m[39m`:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m where `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` invokes the JSON parsing functionality[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - While the harness itself is not the root cause, understanding how test data [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflows into the parser is important for reproduction[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory Allocation Context:**[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The allocation of the [0m[1;36m13[0m[39m-byte buffer and its intended usage[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether the buffer size calculation accounts for null terminators or other [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - String handling and copying operations leading up to line [0m[1;36m327[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Input Processing:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the JSON parser determines buffer sizes based on input[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether there are off-by-one errors in length calculations[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Input validation and sanitization routines[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Important Observations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow is consistently reproducible with the provided test case[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The issue occurs at the exact boundary of the allocated memory, suggesting a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotential off-by-one error[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The [0m[1;36m13[0m[39m-byte allocation size suggests this might be related to a specific JSON [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtoken or string being parsed[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerability involves a READ operation, which while potentially less severe [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthan a WRITE overflow, can still lead to information disclosure or crashes in [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m10[0m[39m:+                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'a'[0m[39m ||[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m11[0m[39m:                             *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'l'[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m's'[0m[39m ||[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m12[0m[39m:                             *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Issue[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe evaluation report identifies a heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability at line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `src/json.c`, occurring in the `json_parse_ex` function during UTF-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m surrogate [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpair parsing. The root cause is a systematic off-by-one error in boundary checking [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore pre-increment dereference operations [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`*++ state.ptr`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability occurs because:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The code uses the pattern `*++ state.ptr`, which first increments the pointer, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthen dereferences it[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The boundary check `end - state.ptr < N` is insufficient when performing N such [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. When `end - state.ptr == N`, the Nth operation will increment `state.ptr` to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mequal `end`, then dereference `*end`, which is out of bounds[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. `end` points to the first byte AFTER the valid buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexclusive boundary[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Specific Issue at Line [0m[1;36m327[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAt line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m327[0m[39m, the code checks `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` before performing [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpre-increment operations:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m operations to verify `\u` sequence[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m operations to read hex digits[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen exactly [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m bytes remain, the 6th operation at line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m increments `state.ptr` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto `end`, then dereferences `*end`, causing the reported [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Systematic Pattern[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAnalysis reveals this is not an isolated bug but a systematic pattern affecting [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocations in the JSON parser. All instances require the same fix: for N consecutive[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`*++ state.ptr` operations, change the boundary check from `end - state.ptr < N` to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`end - state.ptr < N+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mAddresses Evaluation Report[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `src/json.c`, line [0m[1;36m323[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change:** [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Before:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'\\' || [0m[32m([0m[32m*++ state.ptr[0m[32m)[0m[32m != '[0m[39mu' ||[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m After:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'\\' || [0m[32m([0m[32m*++ state.ptr[0m[32m)[0m[32m != '[0m[39mu' ||[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale:** This ensures at least [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes remain before performing [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpre-increment dereference operations, preventing `state.ptr` from reaching or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceeding `end`.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Complete Systematic Fix[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo comprehensively address this vulnerability class, all [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m locations with the same [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern must be fixed:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m** - Unicode escape sequence `\uXXXX` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m operations[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` → `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Context: Parsing basic unicode escape sequences[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m** - UTF-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m surrogate pair `\uXXXX\uYYYY` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m6[0m[39m operations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m **[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mPRIMARY [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFIX[0m[1;39m][0m[39m**[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change: `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` → `end - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Context: Parsing surrogate pairs for characters beyond BMP[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m** - Boolean literal [0m[32m"true"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m operations[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change: `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Context: Parsing the literal value [0m[32m"true"[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m** - Boolean literal [0m[32m"false"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m operations[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change: `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Context: Parsing the literal value [0m[32m"false"[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m** - Null literal [0m[32m"null"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m operations[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change: `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Context: Parsing the literal value [0m[32m"null"[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Apply the primary fix** to line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m to resolve the reported vulnerability[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Apply the systematic fixes** to lines [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m to prevent [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimilar vulnerabilities[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. All changes should be made to the initial codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno previous patches to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreapply[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Each fix changes only the numeric constant in the boundary check condition[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change:** Only modifies boundary check constants, leaving all parsing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic intact[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Correct Semantics:** The fix aligns with the established pattern used [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melsewhere in the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., correct patterns at lines [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m603[0m[39m for [0m[32m"true"[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready exist, just with wrong thresholds[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Side Effects:** Changes are purely defensive checks that prevent buffer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverruns without altering functional behavior[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Systematic:** Addresses the entire class of vulnerability, not just the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreported instance[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- JSON parsing algorithm unchanged[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Unicode escape sequence handling logic preserved[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- UTF-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m surrogate pair decoding logic intact[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Boolean and null literal parsing unchanged[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- String building and memory allocation unaffected[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Error reporting mechanisms preserved[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Two-pass parsing strategy maintained[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issue[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix ensures that before any sequence of N pre-increment dereference operations,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthere are at least N+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m bytes remaining in the buffer. This guarantees that after N [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincrements, `state.ptr < end`, making all dereferences valid.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Specifically for line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m:**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Original: With [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m bytes remaining, 6th increment sets `state.ptr = end`, then [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`*end` overflows[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fixed: With [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes required, when [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m remain the check fails and prevents the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m+ bytes remain, all [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m operations complete safely with `state.ptr < end`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Mitigation of Side Effects[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No functional side effects expected:**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Valid JSON that previously parsed successfully will continue to parse correctly[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Invalid JSON with insufficient bytes will now be properly rejected with error [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmessages[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The existing error handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`goto e_failed` with error message[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Edge cases with exactly N bytes will now correctly fail instead of causing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mundefined behavior[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing compatibility:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Changes are purely defensive bounds checking[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to return values, data structures, or algorithms[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing unit tests should pass unchanged[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzer test cases will verify the fixes prevent the overflow[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix pattern follows the existing style in json.c:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m462[0m[39m uses `state.ptr < [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for lookahead checking[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m281[0m[39m shows the canonical pattern: `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate.ptr == end ? [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m : *state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemonstrates that `end` is exclusive[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The consistent use of `end - state.ptr < N` throughout the file shows this is the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mestablished idiom[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe good patches provided in the vulnerability reports confirm this approach is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect and complete.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
